<Silverscreen> 1,11RANDOM MOVIE TRIVIA: Phoebus' anthropomorphic horse is named Achilles, which leads to two jokes. At one point, Phoebus commands, "Achilles, sit!" - and the horse promptly sits down. The line is a double joke: first, it assumes (correctly, in this case) that the war horse will obey a command normally used for a trained dog. Second, another line is a pun on the phrase "Achilles' heel",
<Silverscreen> 1,11a term for a person's weakness (which itself derives from Achilles in Greek mythology, who was invulnerable except for one heel; the Achilles tendon in the ankle is also named for this).
